# GridNav | API v2.0

Table to work with in-game navigation API.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gridnav#createnpcmap)

CreateNpcMap


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

You should always call \`GridNav.ReleaseNpcMap\` after you done with your build pathing

\`GridNav.CreateNpcMap(\[excluded\_npcs\], \[includeTempTrees\], \[customCollisionSizes\]):\` \[\*\*\`GridNavNpcMap\`\*\*\](GridNavNpcMap.md)

Name

Type

Description

**excluded\_npcs** `**[?]**`

[`**CEntity[]**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/entity)
 | `**nil**`

table with npc to exclude from the map. for example you want to exclude local hero if you build path from local hero position `(default: nil)`

**includeTempTrees** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

`true` if you want include temp trees to the map e.g. furion's 1st spell, iron branch `(default: true)`

**customCollisionSizes** `**[?]**`

`**table**` | `**nil**`

table where key is entity userdata and value is {left, top, right, bottom} offsets from entity position `(default: nil)`

Creates a new `GridNavNpcMap`

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gridnav#releasenpcmap)

ReleaseNpcMap


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GridNav.ReleaseNpcMap(npc_map):` `**nil**`

Name

Type

Description

**npc\_map**

[`**GridNavNpcMap**`arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Boyarinov/gitbook-doc-parser/blob/main/generated/GridNavNpcMap.md)

map to release to release

Releases allocated memory for `GridNavNpcMap`

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gridnav#istraversable)

IsTraversable


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GridNav.IsTraversable(pos, [flag]):` `**boolean**`, `**integer**`

Name

Type

Description

**pos**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

position to check

**flag** `**[?]**`

`**number**`

flag to check `(default: 1)`

Returns `true` if the world position is traversable.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gridnav#buildpath)

BuildPath


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GridNav.BuildPath(start, end_, [ignoreTrees], [npc_map]):` [`**Vector[]**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Name

Type

Description

**start**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

position to start

**end\_**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

position to end

**ignoreTrees** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

`true` if you want to exclude static trees from the pathing `(default: false)`

**npc\_map** `**[?]**`

[`**GridNavNpcMap**`arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Boyarinov/gitbook-doc-parser/blob/main/generated/GridNavNpcMap.md)
 | `**nil**`

map with the npc's positions which works as additional mask for terrain map `(default: nil)`

Build path from start to end. Returns an array with builded positions.

 | `**nil**`

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gridnav#debugrender)

DebugRender


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GridNav.DebugRender([grid_range], [npc_map], [render_cell_flags]):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**grid\_range** `**[?]**`

`**integer**`

grid radius in "cell units" from Vector(0,0,0) `(default: 50)`

**npc\_map** `**[?]**`

[`**GridNavNpcMap**`arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Boyarinov/gitbook-doc-parser/blob/main/generated/GridNavNpcMap.md)
 | `**nil**`

map with the npc's positions which works as additional mask for terrain map `(default: nil)`

**render\_cell\_flags** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

render the flags value for each not approachable cell (don't think you ever want to see this numbers, so ignore this arg) `(default: false)`

Debug render of current GridNav with GridNavNpcMap (if provided)

*   [CreateNpcMap](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gridnav#createnpcmap)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    -- build_path.lua
    return {
        OnUpdate = function()
            local ignore_trees = false;
            local my_hero = Heroes.GetLocal();
            local start_pos = Entity.GetAbsOrigin(my_hero);
            local end_pos = Input.GetWorldCursorPos();
    
            -- create npc map with the temp trees but with no local hero in it
            local npc_map = GridNav.CreateNpcMap({Heroes.GetLocal()}, not ignore_trees);
    
            local path = GridNav.BuildPath(start_pos, end_pos, ignore_trees, npc_map);
            local prev_x, prev_y = nil, nil;
            for i, pos in pairs(path) do
                local x, y, visible = Renderer.WorldToScreen(pos);
                if (prev_x and visible) then
                    Renderer.SetDrawColor(255, 255, 255, 255);
                    Renderer.DrawLine(prev_x, prev_y, x, y);
                end
                prev_x, prev_y = x, y;
            end
    
            -- releasing allocated npc map after we done with build pathing
            GridNav.ReleaseNpcMap(npc_map)
        end
    }
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# GameRules | API v2.0

Table to work with GameRules.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#getpregamestarttime)

GetPreGameStartTime


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Pregame time is the time before the game starts, e.g. ban phase, pick time.

`GameRules.GetPreGameStartTime():` `**number**`

Returns pregame duration or 0 if now is pregame time.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#getgamestarttime)

GetGameStartTime


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Game start time is 0:00 on ingame timer.

`GameRules.GetGameStartTime():` `**number**`

Returns game start time duration or 0 if game is not start yet.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#getgameendtime)

GetGameEndTime


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GameRules.GetGameEndTime():` `**number**`

Returns game end time or 0 if game is not end yet.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#getgameloadtime)

GetGameLoadTime


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GameRules.GetGameLoadTime():` `**number**`

No idea what this function does. Returns 0 in all cases what I've tested.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#getgametime)

GetGameTime


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Can be used to calculate time in an in-game timer. See the example.

`GameRules.GetGameTime():` `**number**`

Returns the current game time. Starts counting from pregame state.

#### 

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#example)

Example

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#ispaused)

IsPaused


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GameRules.IsPaused():` `**boolean**`

Returns `true` if game is paused.

circle-info

GetStockCount


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Item id can be found in \`assets/data/items.json\` file in cheat folder.

\`GameRules.GetStockCount(item\_id, \[team\]):\` \*\*\`integer\`\*\*

Name

Type

Description

**item\_id**

`**integer**`

**team** `**[?]**`

[`**Enum.TeamNum**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/enums#enum.teamnum)

\- Optional. Default is local player's team. `(default: Enum.TeamNum.TEAM_RADIANT)`

Returns amount of remaining items in shop by item id.

#### 

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#example-1)

Example

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/game-engine/gamerules#getnextcycletime)

GetDOTATime


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GameRules.GetDOTATime([pregame], [negative]):` `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**pregame** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

If `true` includes pregame time. `(default: false)`

**negative** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

If `true` includes negative time. `(default: false)`

Returns the actual DOTA in-game clock time.

Copy

    local game_time = GameRules.GetGameTime();
    local ingame_timer = game_time - GameRules.GetGameStartTime();
    Log.Write(string.format("Current time: %d:%02d", math.floor(ingame_timer / 60),
    math.floor(ingame_timer % 60)))

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#directionto)

DirectionTo


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:DirectionTo(other, [dist]):` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Name

Type

Description

**other**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

**dist** `**[?]**`

`**number**`

optional scale factor `(default: 1.0)`

Returns a normalized direction vector from this point to other, optionally scaled by distance. Equivalent to `(other - self):Normalized():Scaled(dist)` but with a single allocation.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#anglebetween2d)

AngleBetween2D


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:AngleBetween2D(middle, point3):` `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**middle**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

the vertex point (this is point1, middle is point2)

**point3**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Returns the angle in radians between two 2D vectors formed by three points. Equivalent to the angle at point2 in the triangle point1-point2-point3, ignoring Z.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#closesttopoint)

ClosestToPoint


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:ClosestToPoint(entities):` [`**CEntity**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/entity)
 | `**nil**`, `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**entities**

[`**CEntity[]**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/entity)

Finds the closest entity to this position from a table of entities. Returns the entity and the distance. Uses Distance2D.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#distancesqr2d)

DistanceSqr2D


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:DistanceSqr2D(other):` `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**other**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Returns the squared 2D distance to another vector. Cheaper than Distance2D (no sqrt). Use for distance comparisons: `a:DistanceSqr2D(b) < range * range`.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#isinrange2d)

IsInRange2D


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:IsInRange2D(other, range):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**other**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

**range**

`**number**`

Returns true if this position is within range of another position (2D, no sqrt).

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#extend2d)

Extend2D


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Extend2D(target, distance):` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Name

Type

Description

**target**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

**distance**

`**number**`

Extends this position towards target by distance (2D, ignores Z). Single allocation. Equivalent to `self + (target - self):Normalized() * distance` without intermediate vectors.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#perpendicular2d)

Perpendicular2D


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Perpendicular2D():` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Returns a 2D perpendicular vector (-y, x, z). Zero allocation if called in-place.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#negate)

Negate


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Negate():` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Negates this vector in-place (-x, -y, -z). Returns self for chaining.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#iszero)

IsZero


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Name

Type

Description

**tolerance** `**[?]**`

`**number**`

`(default: 0.01)`

Returns true if all components are near zero within tolerance.

Extrapolate


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Description

**direction**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

**scalar**

`**number**`

Returns `self + direction * scalar`. Single allocation. Useful for position extrapolation: `start:Extrapolate(velocity, dt * speed)`.

Normalized


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Normalized():` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Returns this vector with a length of 1. When normalized, a vector keeps the same direction but its length is 1.0. Note that the current vector is unchanged and a new normalized vector is returned. If you want to normalize the current vector, use `Vector:Normalize` function.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#normalize)

Normalize


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Normalize():` `**nil**`

Makes this vector have a length of 1. When normalized, a vector keeps the same direction but its length is 1.0. Note that this function will change the current vector. If you want to keep the current vector unchanged, use `Vector:Normalized` function.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#dot)

Dot


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Dot(vector):` `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**vector**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Dot Product of two vectors. The dot product is a float value equal to the magnitudes of the two vectors multiplied together and then multiplied by the cosine of the angle between them. For normalized vectors Dot returns 1 if they point in exactly the same direction, -1 if they point in completely opposite directions and zero if the vectors are perpendicular. [Morearrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@r.w.overdijk/unity-vector3-dot-what-11feb258052e)

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#dot2d)

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#length)

Length


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Length():` `**number**`

Returns the length of this vector. The length of the vector is `math.sqrt(x*x+y*y+z*z)`. If you only need to compare length of some vectors, you can compare squared magnitudes of them using LengthSqr (computing squared length is faster).

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#lengthsqr)

LengthSqr


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:LengthSqr():` `**number**`

Returns the squared length of this vector. This method is faster than Length because it avoids computing a square root. Use this method if you need to compare vectors.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#length2d)

Length2D


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Length2D():` `**number**`

Returns the length of this vector ignoring Z axis.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#length2dsqr)

Length2DSqr


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Length2DSqr():` `**number**`

Returns the squared length of this vector ignoring Z axis. This method is faster than Length2D because it avoids computing a square root. Use this method if you need to compare vectors.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#rotated)

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#lerp)

Lerp


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Lerp(b, t):` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Name

Type

Description

**b**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

end value, returned when t = 1

**t**

`**number**`

value used to interpolate between a and b.

Returns linearly interpolated vector between two vectors. The value returned equals **a + (b - a) \* t** (which can also be written **a \* (1-t) + b\*t**). When `t = 0`, **a:Lerp(b, t)** returns `a`. When `t = 1`, **a:Lerp(b, t)** returns `b`. When `t = 0.5`, **a:Lerp(b, t)** returns the point midway between `a` and `b`.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#cross)

Cross


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`:Cross(vector):` [`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Name

Type

Description

**vector**

[`**Vector**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector)

Returns cross product of two vectors. [Morearrow-up-right](https://docs.unity3d.com/ScriptReference/Vector3.Cross.html)
 [Visualizationarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kz92vvioeng)

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/classes/math/vector#moveforward)

    -- entity position moved forward by 300
    local pos = Entity.GetAbsOrigin(entity):MoveForward(Entity.GetRotation(entity), 300);

# Courier | API v2.0

Table to work with `CCourier`.`**CCourier**` extends `**CNPC**`

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/courier#isflyingcourier)

IsFlyingCourier


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`Courier.IsFlyingCourier(courier):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**courier**

[`**CCourier**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/courier)

The id of the panel or the panel itself to run the script in. `(default: "Dashboard")`

Run a JS script in the panorama context. Return `true` if the script was executed successfully. [JS documentationarrow-up-right](https://developer.valvesoftware.com/wiki/Dota_2_Workshop_Tools/Panorama/Javascript)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    -- in dota console, you should see "Hello from Lua!"
    Engine.RunScript("$.Msg('Hello from Lua!')");

Copy

    -- in dota chat, you should see "Hello from Lua!"
    Engine.ExecuteCommand("say \"Hello from Lua!\"");

Copy

    -- play a sound with a volume of 0.5 (very loud)
    Engine.PlayVol("sounds/npc/courier/courier_acknowledge.vsnd_c", 0.5);

Copy

    Engine.CreateConfig("From lua", {
    {
    	name = "55%+",
    	hero_ids = {1, 2, 3, 4},
    	x = 0.0,
    	y = 0.0,
    	width = 300.0,
    	height = 200.0
    },
    {
    	name = "52%+",
    	hero_ids = {5, 6},
    	x = 350.0,
    	y = 0.0,
    	width = 300.0,
    	height = 200.0
    }
    });

# table | API v2.0

Extensions for the built-in Lua `table` library.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#isempty)

IsEmpty


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.IsEmpty(t):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

Returns true if the table has no entries.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#length)

Length


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Length(t):` `**integer**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

Counts ALL entries (array + hash), unlike `#t` which only counts the sequence part.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#keys)

Keys


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Keys(t):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

Returns a new array containing all keys of the table.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#values)

Values


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Values(t):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

Returns a new array containing all values of the table.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#sum)

Sum


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Sum(t):` `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

Returns the sum of all numeric values in the table. Non-numeric values are skipped.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#reverse)

Reverse


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Reverse(t):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

Returns a new array with the sequence part of `t` in reverse order.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#copyshallow)

CopyShallow


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.CopyShallow(orig, [ignore_mt]):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**orig**

`**table**`

**ignore\_mt** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

If true, the metatable is not copied `(default: false)`

Creates a shallow copy of the table. Copies the metatable unless `ignore_mt` is true.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#copy)

Copy


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Copy(orig):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**orig**

`**table**`

Deep-copies a table with cycle detection. Metatables are preserved.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#kvswap)

KvSwap


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.KvSwap(t, [v_to_true]):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**v\_to\_true** `**[?]**`

`**boolean**`

If true, new values are `true` instead of the original key `(default: false)`

Swaps keys and values. If `v_to_true` is true, all new values become `true` instead of the original key.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#merge)

Merge


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Merge(...):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**...**

`**table**`

Tables to merge

Concatenates array-part entries from all argument tables into a new array.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#mergehm)

MergeHm


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.MergeHm(...):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**...**

`**table**`

Tables to merge

Merges all key-value pairs from argument tables into a new table. Later tables overwrite earlier ones.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#diff)

Diff


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Diff(new_t, old_t):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**new\_t**

`**table**`

**old\_t**

`**table**`

Returns entries in `new_t` whose values differ from `old_t` (compared by rawequal).

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#sorted)

Sorted


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Sorted(t, [compare_func]):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**compare\_func** `**[?]**`

`**fun(a: any, b: any):boolean**`

Optional comparison function

Sorts the table in-place via the built-in `table.sort`, then returns it.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#map)

Map


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Map(t, func):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**func**

`**fun(value: any, key: any):any**`

Callback `func(value, key) -> new_value`

Applies `func(value, key)` to every entry and returns a new array of results.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#filter)

Filter


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Filter(t, func):` `**table**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**func**

`**fun(value: any, key: any):boolean**`

Predicate `func(value, key) -> boolean`

Returns a new array containing only entries for which `func(value, key)` returns true.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#any)

Any


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Any(t, func):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**func**

`**fun(value: any, key: any):boolean**`

Predicate `func(value, key) -> boolean`

Returns true if `func(value, key)` returns true for at least one entry.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#all)

All


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.All(t, func):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**func**

`**fun(value: any, key: any):boolean**`

Predicate `func(value, key) -> boolean`

Returns true if `func(value, key)` returns true for every entry.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#find)

Find


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.Find(t, element):` `**any**`, `**any**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**element**

`**any**`

Element to search for

Finds the first entry matching `element` by raw equality. Returns `value, key` on match, or `nil` if not found.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/table_ext#removeelement)

RemoveElement


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`table.RemoveElement(t, element):` `**boolean**`

Name

Type

Description

**t**

`**table**`

**element**

`**any**` | `**function**`

Element to find or predicate function

Removes the first matching element from the array-part of `t`. If `element` is a function, it is used as a predicate `func(value, index) -> boolean`. Otherwise, finds by raw equality. Shifts remaining elements down to maintain order.

[PreviousGameLocalizerchevron-left](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/gamelocalizer)
[NextStringBuilderchevron-right](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/configuration-and-utilities/stringbuilder)

Description

[`**CItem**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/item)

Returns the game time when the item was purchased. If the item was assembled from other items, It returns the purchase time of the item that had the lowest index at the moment of assembling.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/item#getassembledtime)

GetAssembledTime


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`Item.GetAssembledTime(item):` `**number**`

Name

Type

Description

**item**

[`**CItem**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/item)

Returns the game time when the item was assembled. If the item was not assembled, returns time when the item was purchased.

[hashtag](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/game-components/core/item#purchasedwhiledead)

GetStockCount


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Item id can be found in \`assets/data/items.json\` file in cheat folder.

\`Item.GetStockCount(item\_id, \[team\]):\` \*\*\`integer\`\*\*

Name

Type

Description

**item\_id**

`**integer**`

**team** `**[?]**`

[`**Enum.TeamNum**`](https://uczone.gitbook.io/api-v2.0/cheats-types-and-callbacks/enums#enum.teamnum)

\- Optional. Default is local player's team. `(default: Enum.TeamNum.TEAM_RADIANT)`

Returns amount of remaining items in shop by item id.

    -- set_style.lua
    local css_like_table = {
        ["horizontal-align"] = "center",
    	["vertical-align"] = "center",
        ["transform"] = "translate3d( 0px, -0px, 0px ) scale3d(1, 1, 1)",
        ["padding-left"] = "0px",
        ["margin"] = "0px",
        ["border-radius"] = "4px",
        ["background-color"] = "none",
        ["box-shadow"] = "none",
        ["color"] = "gradient( linear, 0% 100%, 0% 0%, from( #ff00FF ), to( #5C9C68 ) )",
        ["font-size"] = "20px",
        ["text-align"] = "center",
        ["text-decoration"] = "none",
        ["background-size"] = "0% 0%",
        ["opacity-mask"] = 'url("s2r://panorama/images/masks/hudchat_mask_psd.vtex") 1.0',
        ["hue-rotation"] = "-10deg",
        ["text-shadow"] = "2px 2px #111111b0",
        ["blur"] = "gaussian(0px)",
        ["line-height"] = "120%",
        ["font-family"] = "Radiance",
        ["border-brush"] = "gradient( linear, 0% 0%, 0% 100%, from( #96c5ff96 ), to( #12142d2d ) )",
    }
    
    
    local function css_to_string(tbl)
        local str = ""
        for k, v in pairs(tbl) do
            str = str .. k .. ": " .. v .. "; "
        end
        return str;
    end
    
    local health_label = Panorama.GetPanelByName("HealthLabel");
    if (health_label) then
        health_label:SetStyle(css_to_string(css_like_table))
    end
